***rouw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rouw.html>rouw</a> (9342)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:rouwen.html>rouwe</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruwe.html>ruwe</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*reuwa</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hrewwōn</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hrewwō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:pain.html>pain</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sadness.html>sadness</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:regret.html>regret</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:repentance.html>repentance</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hrēow</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rue.html>rue</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Reue</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hryggr</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:more.html>More</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:at.html>at</a> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rue.html>rue</a></span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>noun</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:rouw.html>rouw</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:belongs.html>belongs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>verb</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rouwen.html>rouwen</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rouw.html>rouw</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)

***rozemarijn.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rozemarijn.html>rozemarijn</a> (23701)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">rosmarin</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">rosmarin</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">rōs marīnus</i>. Secondarily influenced <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roos.html>roos</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>rose</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:for.html>for</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:which.html>which</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rosemary.html>rosemary</a></i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruff.html>ruff</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">ruffs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href = vnd.unilang:alternative.html>Alternative</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spelling.html>spelling</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ruffe</i></span></span>: <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:small.html>small</a> freshwater <a href = vnd.unilang:fish.html>fish</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:genus.html>genus</a> <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Gymnocephalus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Gymnocephalus"><i>Gymnocephalus</i></a></span>; <i>specifically</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> Eurasian ruffe (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Gymnocephalus_cernua" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Gymnocephalus cernua"><i>Gymnocephalus cernua</i></a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Gymnocephalus_cernuus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Gymnocephalus cernuus"><i>Gymnocephalus cernuus</i></a></span>) <a href = vnd.unilang:which.html>which</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> spiny <a href = vnd.unilang:fins.html>fins</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pope.html>pope</a></span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">roffle</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">rouffle</i> (earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">romfle</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">ronfle</i>), <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">ronfa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:card.html>card</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:game.html>game</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:similar.html>similar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:whist.html>whist</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <a href = vnd.unilang:these.html>these</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:are.html>are</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:possibly.html>possibly</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">triomphe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:triumph.html>triumph</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:victory.html>victory</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">trionfo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:triumph.html>triumph</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:trump.html>trump</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:card.html>card</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">triumphus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hymn.html>hymn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> Bacchus; <a href = vnd.unilang:celebration.html>celebration</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:triumph.html>triumph</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ultimately.html>ultimately</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">θρῐ́ᾰμβος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">thríambos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hymn.html>hymn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> Dionysius, thriambus</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>verb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> derived <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>noun</a>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rumen</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rūmen</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rūmijaną</i>.
